namespace = shunters

# On_death for Witch Hunter Masters Succession
character_event = {
	id = shunters.1
	hide_window = yes
	picture = GFX_evt_witch_hunters
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_1
			has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_2
			has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_3
	 		has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_4
	 		has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_5
	 		has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_6
	 		has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_7
	 		has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_8
	 		has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_9
	 		has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_10
	 		has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_11
	 		has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_12
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "work event shunters.1"
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_courtier = {
					religion = sigmarite
					trait = witch_hunter
					trait = creature_human
					age = 16
					NOR = {
						trait = incapable
						trait = maimed
						trait = leper
						trait = ill
						trait = has_nurgles_rot
						trait = blinded
						trait = possessed
						trait = lunatic_3
						trait = mutation_minor
						trait = mutation_major
						trait = mutation_massive
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
						trait = magic_potential_1
						trait = magic_potential_2
						trait = magic_potential_3
						trait = magic_potential_4
					}
				}
			}
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					religion = sigmarite
					trait = witch_hunter
					trait = creature_human
					age = 16
					NOR = {
						trait = incapable
						trait = maimed
						trait = leper
						trait = ill
						trait = has_nurgles_rot
						trait = blinded
						trait = possessed
						trait = lunatic_3
						trait = mutation_minor
						trait = mutation_major
						trait = mutation_massive
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
						trait = magic_potential_1
						trait = magic_potential_2
						trait = magic_potential_3
						trait = magic_potential_4
					}
				}
				character_event = {
					id = shunters.10001
				}
			}
			break = yes

		}
		# If no elegible character is aviable, create a new one
		random_list = {
			25 = {
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = RANDOM
					religion = ROOT
					culture = ROOT
					female = no
					age = 35
				}
			}
			25 = {
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = RANDOM
					religion = ROOT
					culture = ROOT
					female = no
					age = 45
				}
			}
			25 = {
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = RANDOM
					religion = ROOT
					culture = ROOT
					female = no
					age = 65
				}
			}
			25 = {
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = RANDOM
					religion = ROOT
					culture = ROOT
					female = yes
					age = 33
				}
			}
		}
		new_character = {
			add_trait = witch_hunter
			add_trait = creature_human
			character_event = {
				id = shunters.10001
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inheritance
character_event = {
	id = shunters.10001
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event shunters.10001"
		FROM = {
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						title = d_witch_hunter_seat_1
						title = d_witch_hunter_seat_2
						title = d_witch_hunter_seat_3
						title = d_witch_hunter_seat_4
						title = d_witch_hunter_seat_5
						title = d_witch_hunter_seat_6
	 		 			title = d_witch_hunter_seat_7
						title = d_witch_hunter_seat_8
						title = d_witch_hunter_seat_9
						title = d_witch_hunter_seat_10
						title = d_witch_hunter_seat_11
						title = d_witch_hunter_seat_12
					}
				}
				grant_title = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

# On_death for Witch Hunter Grand Master Succession
character_event = {
	id = shunters.2
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_landed_title = k_witch_hunters_order
		trait = witch_hunter
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "work event shunters.2"
		299 = {
			province_event = {
				id = shunters.20003 days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

# Ping to province while the randomly selected heir is chosen automatically by Open Elective
province_event = {
	id = shunters.20003
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event shunters.20003"
		any_demesne_title = {
			refill_holding_levy = yes
		}
		k_witch_hunters_order = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = shunters.20002
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inheritance
character_event = {
	id = shunters.20001
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event shunters.20001"
		# if the heir is a Master, clear his seat for a new one.
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_1
					has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_2
					has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_3
					has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_4
					has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_5
				 	has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_6
	 				has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_7
				 	has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_8
	 				has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_9
				 	has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_10
	 				has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_11
				 	has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_12
				}
			}
			character_event = {
				id = shunters.1
			}
		}
		# if the elected party is of a band, destroy the title.
		any_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					title = d_witch_hunter_seat_1
					title = d_witch_hunter_seat_2
					title = d_witch_hunter_seat_3
					title = d_witch_hunter_seat_4
					title = d_witch_hunter_seat_5
				 	title = d_witch_hunter_seat_6
	 				title = d_witch_hunter_seat_7
				 	title = d_witch_hunter_seat_8
	 				title = d_witch_hunter_seat_9
				 	title = d_witch_hunter_seat_10
	 				title = d_witch_hunter_seat_11
				 	title = d_witch_hunter_seat_12
				}
				mercenary = yes
			}
			activate_title = {
				title = THIS status = no
			}
			destroy_landed_title = THIS
		}
		wealth = FROM
		FROM = {
			clear_wealth = THIS
		}
		FROM = {
			abdicate_to = ROOT
		}
		FROM = {
			any_claim = {
				remove_claim = PREV
			}
		}
		any_vassal = {
			remove_title = title_grandmaster_heir
		}
		any_demesne_title = {
			refill_holding_levy = yes
		}
		remove_title = title_grandmaster_heir
	}
}

# The Masters vote (the character receiving this should be the random courtier set as heir)
character_event = {
	id = shunters.20002
	desc = EVTDESCshunters2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_landed_title = k_witch_hunters_order

		log = "work event shunters.20002"
	}

		name = EVTOPTAshunters2
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				8 = {

# On_death for independent Witch Hunters Succession
character_event = {
	id = shunters.3
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	only_rulers = yes

	trigger = {
		trait = witch_hunter
		NOR = {
			has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_1
			has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_2
			has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_3
	 		has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_4
	 		has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_5
	 		has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_6
	 		has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_7
	 		has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_8
	 		has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_9
	 		has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_10
	 		has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_11
	 		has_landed_title = d_witch_hunter_seat_12
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "work event shunters.3"
		IF = {
			limit = {
				government = congregation_government
			}
			set_government_type = congregation_government
			capital_scope = {
				province_event = {
					id = shunters.30003 days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Ping to province while the randomly selected heir is chosen automatically by Open Elective
province_event = {
	id = shunters.30003
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event shunters.30003"
		holder_scope = {
			character_event = {
				id = shunters.30002
			}
			set_government_type = congregation_government
		}
	}
}

# Inheritance
character_event = {
	id = shunters.30001
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event shunters.30001"
 		# if the elected party is of a band, destroy the title.
		any_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				mercenary = yes
			}
			activate_title = {
				title = THIS status = no
			}
			destroy_landed_title = THIS
		}
		wealth = FROM
		FROM = {
			clear_wealth = THIS
		}
		FROM = {
			abdicate_to = ROOT
		}
		FROM = {
			any_claim = {
				remove_claim = PREV
			}
		}
		any_vassal = {
			remove_title = title_knight_captain_heir
		}
		any_courtier = {
			remove_title = title_knight_captain_heir
		}
		any_demesne_title = {
			refill_holding_levy = yes
		}
		remove_title = title_knight_captain_heir
		set_government_type = congregation_government
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = shunters.30002
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event shunters.30002"
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_courtier = {
					religion = sigmarite
					trait = witch_hunter
					trait = creature_human
					age = 16
					has_minor_title = title_knight_captain_heir
					NOR = {
						trait = incapable
						trait = maimed
						trait = leper
						trait = ill
						trait = has_nurgles_rot
						trait = blinded
						trait = possessed
						trait = lunatic_3
						trait = mutation_minor
						trait = mutation_major
						trait = mutation_massive
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
						trait = magic_potential_1
						trait = magic_potential_2
						trait = magic_potential_3
						trait = magic_potential_4
					}
				}
			}
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					religion = sigmarite
					trait = witch_hunter
					trait = creature_human
					age = 16
					has_minor_title = title_knight_captain_heir
					NOR = {
						trait = incapable
						trait = maimed
						trait = leper
						trait = ill
						trait = has_nurgles_rot
						trait = blinded
						trait = possessed
						trait = lunatic_3
						trait = mutation_minor
						trait = mutation_major
						trait = mutation_massive
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
						trait = magic_potential_1
						trait = magic_potential_2
						trait = magic_potential_3
						trait = magic_potential_4
					}
				}
				character_event = {
					id = shunters.30001
				}
			}
			break = yes

		}
		# If no elegible character is aviable, create a new one
		random_list = {
			25 = {
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = RANDOM
					religion = ROOT
					culture = ROOT
					female = no
					age = 35
				}
			}
			25 = {
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = RANDOM
					religion = ROOT
					culture = ROOT
					female = no
					age = 45
				}
			}
			25 = {
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = RANDOM
					religion = ROOT
					culture = ROOT
					female = no
					age = 65
				}
			}
			25 = {
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = RANDOM
					religion = ROOT
					culture = ROOT
					female = yes
					age = 33
				}
			}
		}
		new_character = {
			add_trait = witch_hunter
			add_trait = creature_human
			character_event = {
				id = shunters.30001
			}
		}
	}
}
